- [Montenégra Adire Heavyweight Fleece Hoodie](https://montenegra-london.com/products/essential-heavyweight-fleece-hoodie): The Montenégra Adire Essential Heavyweight Fleece Hoodie represents the foundation of the Montenégra uniform. Reduced to form, weight, and intention, the piece embodies brutal minimalism through proportion rather than decoration. Designed as an everyday constant, the silhouette balances structure with comfort. Dropped shoulders and a relaxed oversized profile create quiet presence, allowing movement without excess. The hoodie exists not as trend driven streetwear but as a permanent layer within a modern wardrobe. Constructed from heavyweight cotton blend fleece, the fabric delivers warmth, durability, and a substantial hand feel while maintaining softness against the body. Heavyweight fleece garments are valued within luxury streetwear for their longevity and structured drape, forming essential year round staples within contemporary wardrobes. This is clothing distilled to necessity. Design and Construction Heavyweight fleece cotton blend construction Approx. 350gsm fabric weight for structure and warmth Oversized unisex silhouette Dropped shoulder design Fixed hood with functional coverage Front pouch pocket Ribbed cuffs and hem for stability Designed for daily wear across seasons The dense fleece composition provides insulation while maintaining breathable comfort, allowing the garment to transition between layering and standalone wear. Fit and Styling Engineered for a relaxed oversized fit. Wear true to size for a contemporary streetwear silhouette or size down for a cleaner structured profile. Designed to pair effortlessly with boxy tees, tailored trousers, or cargos as part of the Montenégra modern uniform. The Montenégra Uniform Montenégra creates garments intended to accompany the journey inward. Each essential removes distraction until only presence remains. The Essential Heavyweight Hoodie functions as armour in motion. A foundational piece within ACT I, guiding the wearer closer to Montenégra. The return to the mountain begins with simplicity.
